CREATE TABLE Media_Directors (media_id INT, director_name VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (media_id) REFERENCES Media(id))</t><stat>UPSERT INTO Media_Genres (media_id, genre_name) VALUES (1, 'Action') ON CONFLICT (media_id, genre_name) DO NOTHING</stat><divider><t>CREATE TABLE Media_Actors (media_id INT, actor_name VARCHAR(255), FOREIGN KEY (media_id) REFERENCES Media(id))

);
